< Review>
My entire experience with these guys was excellent. I'm always paranoid when it comes to my things so it took me months before I actually trusted them enough to clean my console! LOL but when I finally was ready they gave me a quote and set me up with an appointment a couple days later which I thought was very quick.
I already misplaced the business cards that I was given but if I remember correctly my technicians name was Alex?. I met him in a shopping center and quickly got down to brass tacks! He asked me what problems I was having with it and I mentioned to him that I wasn't really having any issues it just got really hot and I've had it for around for years and I just wanted to clean it out before anything goes wrong. Suffice to say I made the appointment for a cleaning.

So I nervously handed over my PS4 and waiting in my car for him to get started. Around 10-15 minutes later he ended up telling me that after opening up my PS4 he found that it wasn't actually dirty. I'm proud to say he said it was rather clean but here's the good part. And objectively yes this might be a tactic I don't know but I trusted the guy. Even though he opened up my PS4 for a cleaning which is what I was supposed to be charged for the ended up telling me that he wasn't going to charge me for a cleaning because there wasn't much to clean and I really appreciated that. He actually tried to discern what the problem was and proceeded to fix it. He told me the thermal pasting inside of the PlayStation is what was causing it to get a little hot in that mine was reaching the end of its life and there was barely any left. He told me since the problem wasn't with the cleaning if I wanted he could just charge me for the thermal pasting which was twenty bucks more but in my opinion if it prolong the life of my PlayStation and makes it so I don't have to buy another console for another year at least then that was fine with me. Any other company would have charged you the $60 for cleaning even if it wasn't dirty so I appreciate these guys for actually caring. Sure I ended up paying 20 bucks more than what I expected but the fact is they tried to figure out what the problem was. I'm not sure if $80 is an average price for a thermal pasting butt feel free to do your own research on that. I trusted my technician and as we speak I'm playing it with no issues. It still gets a little warm and loud at the start-up of the game I play dead by daylight. But all in all I texted Alex to let him know and he said that was perfectly normal. Time will tell. As far as I'm concerned I'm satisfied. Thank you Tech Cidents< /Review>

<response>None< /response>< Text>
I played the course for the first time while visiting family on Friday September 16.  The course was in overall good shape.  Some of the greens are very big with nice curves.  Noted the lip of the cups were not groomed which caused several missed putts. You have to hit almost dead center to sink a putt.  Also noted numerous ball marks and debris on the greens that needed repair to no fault of the course greens keeper.  (Fix your ball marks guys and gals!!)    Front nine featured some very narrow fairways which proved unfriendly to a fade or draw.  The back nine opened up some and the water holes provided a fair challenge.  Overall I would play the course again when in the area.  A suggestion would be to provide a map of the course, of some signage, that would assist a person, not from the area, with finding the holes on the back nine.  Had to use a number of paved streets to navigate and if I were not with a local, I would still be lost.<//Text>

< Review>
Somehow someone keeps deleting my post - so here we go again.

This review is strickly regarding the food service and food quality:   My mother has been at Lifehouse for about 20 days (for rehabilitation purposes).   Lifehouse puts out a weekly menu for breakfast, lunch and dinner.  We make sure that a family member is present for each meal.   Not ONCE has my mother received the entire meal that is outlined on the printed menu.  My mom is not on a restricted diet. There is ALWAYS something missing (i.e. salad, soup, condiments, dinner roll, ENTREE etc....).  Most of the time she is served something completely different than the entree outlined on the menu (i.e. cold roast beef sandwich in place of a hot entree or oatmeal in place of an omelette).   On three occassions I had to ask for silverware.... yes, they forget to bring silverware witht he meal.  I spoke with the Charge Nurse and she said my mother could order a "special" meal.   My mother does not need to order a "special" meal, she just needs to be served the entree on the menu.  The weekly menu is a great idea.  We were able to bring mom food from home for those meals we knew she would not like.  We now bring all her meals from home since we can't depend on Lifehouse for satisfactory meals.   My mother will ask "what about the omelette" and the server will say "oh, did you want the omelette?"  sometimes the server will leave and return with the requested item and sometimes they leave and never return.  We are paying good money for mom to be in this place.  It they can't stick to the printed menu... well, why put one out?   Please check on your loved one's.... especially at meal time.   One server told me they "ran out" of the breakfast omelette.    What??? ran out??   this is not a restaurant, they know in advance how many people they are serving.   My mother has been served a cold sandwich for the past 4 dinners, twice it was only half a sandwich.... This is UNACCEPTABLE.  At first I thought maybe mom was being served someone else's menu.... sadly this was not the case.   We now bring all her meals from home.   Our family never expected 5 star meals, however, we did expect edible well balanced meals.  I agree with the other post regarding the sandwiches.... they truly are horrible.

Just something to consider if you are considering Lifehouse.<//Review>

I have been going to this gym now for a few months.  I have tried to come in the mornings, afternoons and evenings.
